 According to a report by zdnet, group-ib has said that the details of these cards are being sold for $ 100
 havers aam taur par balk main card ditels kharidte hai or phir inhen ek ek karke yuj karte hai or safal hone par un cards main kuch ke acounts khaali kar dete hai
 However, the source of the card is not known from where it was brought
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki shuruaati analysis ye baat saamne aa rahi he ATM or pos system main install kiye skimming divaais se colect kiye gaye hai
 Talking about skimming, this is one way that fraud collects cardholder details
 is methd ke tahat ek chota divaais ATM yaa pos mashin main lagaaya jaataa he
 It is worth noting that the information of 12 lakh debit credit cards uploaded on the website contains the data which is on the magnetic strip of the payment card
 is tarah kaa data bhi skimming methd ke tahat colect kiya ja saktaa he
 According to the report, all these Indian card details have been uploaded on Joker Stash, which is a popular dark web destination for payment card data
 yahaan se frods cards kii ditels kharidte hai or ise ATM se paise nikaalane ke liye card chloning karte hai
 How can you avoid this kind of data theft? There are some guidelines which banks often tell you via message or call
 kisi bhi debit yaa credit card ko kisi atm main yuj karne se pehle us atm kii thik se jaanch kar len
 Check that there is no device attached
 sunsaan jagah ke atm yaa phir aisa atm jise dekh kar aapako lag rahaa he ki iske saath ched chhaad kii gai he yaa kisi tarah se nuksaan pahunchaaya gaya he, isamen ATM card na daalen

 inamen firozabad, jasrana, shikohabad, sirsaganj or toundla shaamil hai

 2012 main sapa ne yahaan se om prakaash verma ko khadaa kiya jinhone bispi ke mukesh verma par badi jeet hasil kii

 agra kaint se pichley teen chunaavon main lagaataar bispi ke candidet vijayi rahe hai jabaki agra north se bijepi ke jagan prasad garg 2002 se vidhayak hai

 ) uttar pradesh kii fatehpur loksabhaa seat ek daur main soobe kii nahin balki desh kii hai profile siton main shumaar kii jaati thi
 VP Singh became the Prime Minister of the country by winning elections from Janata Dal from here
 fatehpur soobe kaa prachin shaharon main se ek he, jiskaa zikr puraanon main miltaa he
 In Vedic period, it was also called as inland, which means such a fertile area which is situated between two rivers
 fatehpur loksabhaa seat ganga or yamuna ke bich basaa hua he
 From Congress to SP, BSP and BJP, the public has won the election
 maujuuda samay main fatehpur seat par bijepi kaa kabja he
 Political background: Fatehpur Lok Sabha seat has been held 16 times since independence
 inamen se sabase zyada 5 baar congress ko jeet mili he
 While BJP (3 times), Janata Dal (twice), BSP (twice), SP (once), Lok Dal (once), independent candidates have also won
 fatehpur seat par pehali baar 1957 main loksabhaa chunaav hua tha, jisamen congress ke ansaar harvani chunaav jitkar saansad bane
 After this, Gauri Shankar Kakkar was elected as an independent candidate in the elections in 1962
 lekin 1967 main congress ne vaapasi kii 1971 ke chunaav main jeet hasil karne main kaamyaab rahi
 In 1977, Bashir Ahmed defeated the Congress from the Bharatiya Lok Dal and managed to win the Liaquat Hussain of the Janata Party in the 1978 by-election
 haalanki, iske baad 1980 main congress ne phir vaapasi or lagaataar do chunaav jeetne main kaamyaab rahi
 In the 1989 Lok Sabha elections, VP Singh descended from the Janata Dal and became the Prime Minister of the country
 wo is seat se do baar saansad chune gaye
 Vishambhar Prasad Nishad won from the BSP in 1996, but in the 1998 elections, the BJP managed to feed the lotus
 yahaan se ashok kumaar patel lagaataar do baar bijepi se saansad chune gaye

 2009 main samaajawaadee party ke rakesh sachaan saansad chune gaye
 After this, in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, Niranjan Jyoti of BJP was elected MP here and became a minister in the Modi government

 yah baat alag he ki sarkaar is anivaaryta ko swikaarne se dar rahi he
 The reorganization of the railway after the budget-merger should have four dimensions: First: Through accounting reforms, the social responsibilities and commercial business of the railways have to be separated and budget subsidies will be set for selected social services and projects
